Confirmed: (1) never-raise holds (every public entry and helper is try/except -> None; verified bad-image, provider-None, garbage-JSON, bad-pitch-in-chord all return None without raising); (2) gating is byte-identical with no key (`llm_available()` False -> `process_job` takes the existing path), and a FAST scan skips the LLM (test `test_llm_skipped_on_fast_scan` raises if transcribe runs); (3) the deterministic builder is correct: `<backup>` == staff-1 total (both `_staff_total` and `_build_event` map non-positive durations to 1, so they always agree), chords collapse to one onset with `<chord/>` members in valid element order, a bad FIRST chord pitch is dropped and the next pitch correctly becomes the onset (not a chord member), attributes emit only in measure 1, 1-part output no-ops through merge_to_grand_staff + normalize_ties; (4) PDF fallback hazard is safe: `rasterize_if_pdf` PDF branch does NOT rename/consume `input_path` (it reads the PDF, writes stitched.png), so Clarity can still read the PDF on fallback; the non-PDF LLM path passes `input_path` directly (no rename) so the fallback `rasterize_if_pdf` PNG branch still finds it; (5) security: zero logging in llm_omr (key never printed; only job_id logged in worker), `OMR_LLM_BASE_URL`/`OMR_LLM_PROVIDER` are env-only (not request-controlled) so SSRF is operator-trust only, image is user-data but only enters the POST body (not the URL) and output is parsed JSON->MusicXML defensively so prompt-injection blast radius is "garbage JSON -> None -> fallback", no secrets in repo, stdlib-only (urllib/json/base64) + PIL (existing dep). NON-BLOCKING gaps recorded for follow-up: (a) `_encode_image` does NOT arm Pillow's `Image.MAX_IMAGE_PIXELS` decompression-bomb guard the way `stitch_pages_vertical` does, so a crafted non-PDF image on the LLM path could spike memory during decode (mitigated: inert by default + try/except catches DecompressionBombError -> None; fix: set `Image.MAX_IMAGE_PIXELS = MAX_STITCH_PIXELS` before `Image.open` in `_encode_image`); (b) `max_tokens: 8192` can truncate JSON on a large multi-page score -> parse fail -> clean fallback, a quality ceiling not a safety bug; (c) PDF fallback re-rasterizes (LLM rasterizes, then `_select_*` rasterizes again) - correct but wasteful, could cache the stitched path. 184 pytest / 339 JS green on the branch.

- **2026-06-03 - NEW ENGINE: LLM-vision transcriber (`omr-worker/llm_omr.py`), the "big value, low latency" direction. Default OMR (when configured) becomes a single vision-LLM call that reads the score image holistically, incl. CHORDS (the case Clarity/oemer/referee structurally cannot fix). Ships INERT (no key = no behavior change). Branch `feat/omr-llm-transcriber`.** Rationale (user decision, after the ensemble+referee proved small-accuracy-for-big-latency): a multimodal LLM is robust to chords/dense polyphony and returns in seconds (one API round-trip) vs oemer's 3-7min, so it can be both more accurate AND lower latency. This consciously relaxes the "free tooling" hard rule (opt-in, ~pennies/scan); it stays free by default because the engine is inert without a key.
  - **Module:** `transcribe(image_path) -> MusicXML bytes | None` (NEVER raises). Provider-agnostic via tiny stdlib-urllib adapters (anthropic default / openai / gemini), NO new pip dep. The LLM returns a STRICT JSON note model (per measure: staff1/staff2 event lists; an event is a rest or a {duration, pitches[]} where a CHORD lists all its pitches together); `score_json_to_musicxml` then DETERMINISTICALLY builds a 1-part/2-staff grand staff (oemer's shape) so the output is always well-formed and flows through merge_to_grand_staff + normalize_ties unchanged. The JSON->MusicXML builder is PURE + unit-tested (incl. the icarus-style 3-note bass chord -> one onset, two `<chord/>` members).
  - **Worker wiring (`process_job`):** `if llm_omr.llm_available() and not fast: try transcribe; if bytes -> use them (source "llm"), else fall through` to the existing ensemble/legacy path. So precedence is LLM (when keyed) -> ensemble (if OMR_ENSEMBLE) -> legacy Clarity. A FAST scan skips the LLM (no API cost) and takes the free Clarity-only path. `llm_available()` = `OMR_LLM` truthy AND a provider key present, so prod is byte-identical to today until a key is set. For a PDF the existing `rasterize_if_pdf` makes the image (leaves the PDF intact for the fallback engines); a non-PDF image is sent directly.
  - **Env:** `OMR_LLM=1` + `OMR_LLM_PROVIDER` (anthropic|openai|gemini) + a key (`OMR_LLM_API_KEY` or the provider-standard `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY`/`OPENAI_API_KEY`/`GEMINI_API_KEY`). Optional: `OMR_LLM_MODEL`, `OMR_LLM_BASE_URL`, `OMR_LLM_MAX_EDGE` (image long-edge px, cost lever, default 2048), `OMR_LLM_TIMEOUT`.
  - **Tests:** `test_llm_omr.py` (15: chord builder, rests/alters, attributes/2-staff/backup, garbage->None, JSON-fence extraction, gating, never-raise, fake-provider end-to-end) + `test_worker.py` (+4: LLM used when available+not-fast, skipped on fast, falls back on None, off-by-default). 339 JS + 184 pytest green.
  - **STILL TO VALIDATE (the acceptance test):** with a real key set on the cx33, confirm it gets the icarus 4th-measure bass CHORD right (the documented failure the ensemble+referee could not fix), then a broader real-photo/PDF accuracy + cost pass. NOT enabled in prod yet (no key). Open follow-ups: multi-page handling (currently one stitched image downscaled to OMR_LLM_MAX_EDGE), rhythm/duration accuracy, and a cost/latency measurement at real volume.

- **2026-06-03 - "FAST SCAN" per-job opt-out shipped + ensemble enablement plan. Default OMR is now the full ensemble (Clarity + oemer + referee, most accurate); users can tick "Fast scan" to skip oemer for a ~5x faster single-engine result.** Branch `feat/omr-fast-scan-toggle`. The latency cost of the ensemble is NOT parallelism (Clarity + oemer already run concurrently via `run_primary_engines`); it is that oemer is intrinsically ~3-7min on CPU vs Clarity's ~1min, plus 4-vCPU contention, so wall-clock ~= max(slowed engines) ~= 3-5x the Clarity-only short-circuit (icarus 79s->~7min, the_cut 211s->633s). The toggle gives users the choice rather than forcing the slow path.
  - **Mechanism (per-job flag, NOT a global env):** UI checkbox `#fast-scan` (index.html, default OFF=accurate) -> `submitOmr(file, {fast})` (src/omr.ts) appends form field `fast=1` -> `functions/api/omr.ts` sets R2 `customMetadata: {fast:"1"}` on the upload object -> `worker.job_is_fast()` reads it via `head_object` `Metadata['fast']` (botocore lowercases keys; R2 customMetadata surfaces as S3 x-amz-meta-*) -> `process_job` branches `if ensemble_enabled() and not fast: _select_ensemble else: _select_legacy`. `job_is_fast` defaults to False (accurate) on any read failure, so a metadata hiccup never silently downgrades quality. Tests: src/omr.test.ts (+1 fast form field), omr-worker/test_worker.py (+3: job_is_fast spellings/never-raise, fast-takes-legacy-even-with-ensemble-on, default-runs-ensemble), src/omr-worker.test.ts structural guard updated to the new branch. 339 JS + 165 pytest green.
  - **ENABLEMENT:** this needs (a) the frontend+function via Cloudflare Pages (auto on merge) AND (b) the worker.py change deployed to the cx33 (`cd /opt/piano-helper && sudo -u ubuntu git fetch && git reset --hard origin/main` + `systemctl restart omr-worker`) AND (c) setting `OMR_ENSEMBLE=1` + `OMR_ENSEMBLE_REFEREE=1` in `/etc/piano-helper-omr.env`. Order matters: deploy worker.py + flip env TOGETHER so the per-job fast flag is honored the moment the ensemble becomes the default (no "all-slow-no-escape" window; before the box deploy the frontend toggle is simply inert and everything stays the fast Clarity-only path). Persist the env flags in the deploy mechanism, not just the live file, or a redeploy resets them.

- **2026-06-03 - SPIKE (throwaway, cx33): CLARITY-ONLY visual PDF self-verification (an oemer-free referee). Verdict: UNCERTAIN, leaning NO for now - the SCORER works oemer-free but oemer-free LOCALIZATION is an unsolved sub-problem. Do NOT build the production module until a localizer spike clears.** The motivation: the referee's accuracy is inseparable from oemer's latency (it needs oemer's competing pitch AND oemer's notehead bbox), so an oemer-free "compare Clarity's output to the input PDF directly" path would be high-accuracy + low-latency. Findings: (1) SCORING half = solid PASS. Using `referee.score_candidate` on the icarus m15 ground-truth misread (Clarity E6, truth C6), C6 is the top scorer and beats E6 by margin 0.25 (threshold 0.10), on BOTH oemer's working raster AND an independent pdftoppm 350-DPI raster (raster-source independent). False-flag check across 24 correctly-read isolated notes (icarus + Reverie): 0/24 wrong flips at the 0.10 gate (dense Reverie came within ~0.04 but the gate absorbed it). (2) LOCALIZATION half = the BLOCKER. Verovio renders Clarity's MusicXML and pins every notehead to pixel coords, BUT verovio re-engraves with its OWN line-breaking/margins (1 page/4 systems vs the input PDF's 3 systems/page, first staff y=143 vs 616), so global render-to-input registration is off by entire systems - far beyond the ~12px (half-staff-space @350DPI) tolerance. Y is recoverable from the input's own staff lines; the unsolved part is the per-measure X mapping (input barline segmentation was noisy: stems/braces mixed with true barlines) - i.e. reconstructing the per-note structural index that oemer already provides. RISK if pursued naively: a localization error of one staff-step crops the wrong note and the scorer (no second engine) confidently "corrects" to a wrong pitch; the decline gate guards pitch ambiguity, not crop-position error. NEXT (only if revisited): a localization-only spike (input staff-line + notehead-blob detection, X via barline-segmented measures) measured against the cached oemer bbox index as ground truth across all 4 PDFs; greenlight only if it hits <= half-a-staff-space reliably.

- **2026-06-03 - ENSEMBLE OMR SLICE 6d: align() OPTIMAL-ASSIGNMENT pairing + referee DENSE-RUN decline-guard. RE-VALIDATED on the 4 real PDFs = 0 REGRESSIONS (Reverie 13 -> 0). The visual-diff referee is now never-worse on the validated set; ships DEFAULT-OFF still (the env flag-flip is a separate QA-gated slice).** Branch `fix/omr-align-optimal-assignment`. Fixes the Slice-6c blocker above in TWO layers.
  - **Layer 1 - `align()` pairing (`omr-worker/reconcile.py`, `_match_cell` now `_match_cell_optimal`):** replaced GREEDY nearest-onset matching with a GLOBAL minimal-cost MAXIMUM-cardinality assignment (pure-stdlib Hungarian, `_hungarian`) per (measure,staff) cell, keyed on BOTH onset and pitch: cost = `pitch_distance*(eps+1) + onset_distance`, so pitch agreement DOMINATES onset proximity inside the eps window. Greedy crossed a swapped within-eps pair into two phantom A->B/B->A disputes; the optimal assignment pairs like-pitch with like-pitch so they AGREE (no dispute, no referee). Greedy kept as `_match_cell_greedy`, the never-raise fallback (`_match_cell` try/excepts to it). Hungarian verified optimal vs brute force over 35k random matrices. Buckets contract (matched/only_a/only_b) unchanged; stdlib-only; never-raises.
  - **Layer 2 - the ACTUAL Reverie fix (`_dense_run_slots`):** Layer 1 alone did NOT clear Reverie. Re-validation showed the 13 regressions are NOT within-eps greedy crossing: they are ENGINE-LEVEL note-ORDER drift across a FULL EIGHTH (the swapped notes are 5040 ticks apart, quarter=10080, far beyond eps=1260). The two engines disagree on the temporal ORDER of two distinct-pitch notes in a beamed run, so a Clarity note is matched to the oemer note at the SAME onset but a DIFFERENT physical position; the position-based referee crops by oemer's order-drifted bbox, sees a real-but-wrong-slot notehead, and confidently confirms the swap. This is EXACTLY what Slice 5's GO/NO-GO said to DECLINE ("dense/beamed regions"), but the wiring only checked single-note-per-slot ISOLATION, which every eighth in a run passes. `_dense_run_slots` flags any slot whose nearest same-cell pitched neighbor is `< one quarter` (e.base ticks) away; the referee gate now requires `is_isolated and not is_dense`. An isolated QUARTER-note dispute (neighbors a full quarter apart) still reaches the referee, so the Icarus E6->C6 correction survives. Belt-and-suspenders `_referee_onset_coincides` also declines when a matched pair's onsets don't coincide (within half-eps).
  - **RE-VALIDATION (cx33 .venv311, `OMR_ENSEMBLE=1 OMR_ENSEMBLE_REFEREE=1` vs Clarity baseline; isolated `/tmp/align-val`, live systemd service + R2 env UNTOUCHED; driver mirrors `_select_ensemble`/`_reconcile_paths`, diffs Clarity vs reconciled in document order):** icarus **1 change m15 E6->C6 = CORRECTION** (ground-truthed against the composer's `icarus.mscz`: m15 treble = C6 E6 F6 E6, first note IS C6; Clarity misread it E6); Liminality **2 changes** (m31/m32 staff-2 4-note CHORD, the pre-existing class-B DIATONICITY heuristic Eb->E / F#->G, NOT the referee - chords fail the isolation gate - and in a region where Clarity is already wrong vs the truth {C3,E3,G3}, so neutral, not a regression of a correct note); **Reverie 0 changes (was 13 - the swap-pair regressions are GONE)**; the_cut **0 changes** (was 1; its m55 E5->G5 quarter sits in a dense pocket so the guard now declines - conservative). NO notes lost on any score. NET across 4 PDFs: 1 verified correction, 0 regressions. Tests: `test_reconcile.py` +7 (dense swapped-run pairs by pitch, cardinality-then-best-pitch, lone octave still matches as class B, Hungarian brute-force sanity, decline-guard, dense-run detector); 161 passed / 15 skipped (verovio tier skips cleanly).
  - **ENABLE STATUS: referee stays DEFAULT-OFF in this slice.** The deliverable allows flipping `OMR_ENSEMBLE`/`OMR_ENSEMBLE_REFEREE` on only after the QA role confirms the live feature in a browser; that env flag-flip on the cx33 worker is a separate small slice, not this code PR. The code is now safe (0 regressions on the validated set); the remaining risk is scores unlike these 4 (the referee only fires on isolated, non-dense, >=third pitch disputes and declines otherwise, so the floor is Clarity).

- **2026-06-02 - ENSEMBLE OMR SLICE 6c: oemer-bbox REFEREE LOCALIZATION built + end-to-end validated on 4 real PDFs (branch `feat/omr-referee-localize-bbox`). SHIPS DEFAULT-OFF; the referee is NOT safe to enable yet.** The Slice-6b localization blocker is removed for the OEMER candidate: `omr-worker/oemer_bbox.py` runs oemer as a LIBRARY (not the CLI) to capture a per-note bbox index (notehead bbox + 5 staff-line y's in oemer's working-image space), threaded `run_oemer` -> `_select_ensemble` -> `_reconcile_paths` -> `reconcile(input_pdf=artifact)`. `reconcile._localize_dispute` + `_bbox_row_for` crop the disputed oemer note for `referee_pick`. All gated behind `OMR_ENSEMBLE_REFEREE`; any capture failure falls back to the plain oemer CLI (engine result never regresses); flag/sub-gate OFF = byte-identical to Slice 4. Tests: `test_reconcile.py` +8 synthetic-artifact localization tests (no oemer/verovio). END-TO-END VALIDATION (cx33 .venv311, `OMR_ENSEMBLE=1 OMR_ENSEMBLE_REFEREE=1`, vs Clarity baseline; driver `/tmp/referee_val.py`, isolated `/tmp/referee-val`, live service untouched): icarus 1 change (E6->C6, likely correct - C6 recurs in that passage), the_cut 1 change / 513 notes, Liminality 4, **Reverie 13 changes = REGRESSIONS**. NO notes ever lost on any score. **THE BLOCKER (root cause, the next fix):** on DENSE eighth-note runs (Reverie), `align()` pairs a Clarity note with the WRONG neighboring oemer note (onset tolerance `EPS_BEATS` merges neighbors), so the referee faithfully crops oemer's neighbor and confidently CONFIRMS the swapped pitch (verified: it relabeled a clearly-above-staff G5 as B4). Signature = adjacent A->B / B->A swap PAIRS. The margin guard cannot catch it (the crop really contains that wrong note). The referee VISION is sound (octave 30/30; icarus/the_cut conservative); the failure is upstream PAIRING. FIX DIRECTION: make `align()` robust in dense runs, or DECLINE when a pair can't be unambiguously matched (e.g. localize Clarity's candidate too and require both candidates' x-positions to coincide; or decline inside beamed runs). Re-validate Reverie before any enable.**

- **2026-06-02 - ENSEMBLE OMR RECONCILE CORRECTNESS FIX (branch `fix/omr-reconcile-conservative`, NO PR yet): GROUND-TRUTH QA against the composer's real Icarus `.mscz` (a clean C-major piece) found `reconcile()` made 3 REGRESSIONS and 0 CORRECTIONS. Two root causes, both fixed in `omr-worker/reconcile.py`. The fix makes class B never-worse-than-Clarity on clean diatonic input: with no strong positive signal, class B makes ~0 changes.**
  - **DEFECT 1 (the culprit for the regressions) - the voice-leading override was UNSAFE.** `_vote_pitch`'s class-B chain had a voice-leading branch ("smaller melodic interval from the previous same-staff note wins") and an octave/tessitura branch. On clean input where Clarity is correct, voice-leading OVERRODE correct Clarity readings with oemer's wrong pitch (e.g. it preferred oemer's nearer-interval B for a correct Clarity note). FIX: REMOVED both the voice-leading branch AND the octave/tessitura branch from `_vote_pitch`. The ONLY signals that can now override the Clarity primary are (a) range hard-reject (out of MIDI 21..108) and (b) key-signature diatonicity (oemer diatonic AND Clarity non-diatonic -> oemer). Everything else tiebreaks to Clarity. `_pitch_vote_is_residual` was updated to mirror the new branch order (residual = both in range AND both diatonic-or-both-not); the octave-jump + voice-leading branches were removed from it too. `prev_midi` is kept on both signatures for compatibility but is now unused; `_STAFF_TESSITURA` is left defined but unused.
  - **DEFECT 2 - duplicate-pitch bug in the class-B application path.** When the vote picked oemer, `_apply_pitch` could swap a chord member's pitch onto a pitch ANOTHER member of the same chord/onset already had, emitting an invalid chord with two identical pitches (e.g. {C2,G#2} where the G#2 member, non-diatonic, was diatonicity-corrected to a C2 that the chord already contained -> {C2,C2}). FIX: a DUPLICATE GUARD at the call site. New pure helper `_onset_slot_midis(events)` maps `(measure,staff,onset) -> set of Clarity MIDI pitches`; before applying a pitch swap, if oemer's new pitch is already present at that slot in ANOTHER note (slot pitches minus the note's own), DECLINE the swap and keep Clarity. Never emit a chord with two identical pitches.
  - **Tests (`test_reconcile.py`):** added the 4 QA-derived regression tests: (a) `test_class_b_keeps_clarity_chord_when_both_diatonic` (clean chord G3+C4+E4, oemer reads B3 for C4 -> KEEP Clarity's C4, both diatonic so no override); (b) `test_class_b_declines_swap_that_would_duplicate_chord_pitch` ({C2,G#2}, diatonicity wants G#2->C2 but C2 already present -> DECLINE, stays {C2,G#2}); (c) `test_class_b_genuine_diatonicity_correction_still_applies` (lone F#4 vs diatonic F4 in C major -> oemer F4 still wins, the good signal survives); (d) range-reject already covered by `test_class_b_range_rejects_out_of_range`. UPDATED two tests that asserted the OLD voice-leading behavior: `test_class_b_voice_leading_picks_nearer_pitch` -> `test_class_b_voice_leading_no_longer_overrides_clarity` (now KEEPS Clarity), and `test_pitch_vote_is_residual_false_when_voice_leading_decides` -> `test_pitch_vote_is_residual_ignores_voice_leading` (voice-leading no longer makes a dispute non-residual). RESULTS: base env (no verovio) 147 passed + 15 skipped (referee verovio tier); `/tmp/verovio-spike` venv 162 passed (referee tier runs; the E5-vs-G5 residual is still in scope). Slice-6b referee behavior unchanged: its residual fixtures are both-diatonic-in-range so they remain residual under the new predicate. No JS/build touched.**

- **2026-06-02 - ENSEMBLE OMR SLICE 6b WIRED: the visual-diff referee (`referee.py`, on main via #153) is now plumbed into `reconcile()` as the RESIDUAL class-B tiebreaker behind its OWN sub-gate `OMR_ENSEMBLE_REFEREE` (default OFF, also requires OMR_ENSEMBLE). Branch `feat/omr-referee-wire` off origin/main, NO PR yet. Heuristics run FIRST; the referee is consulted ONLY when the free pitch vote could not separate the pair AND the dispute is in the referee's proven scope. Flag OFF / sub-gate OFF = byte-identical to Slice 4 (verified). LOCALIZATION TOOK FALLBACK PATH (b): the localizer returns None today (correct no-op), so the referee always declines; robust note localization is the documented remaining blocker (details below).**
  - **THE LOCALIZATION DECISION (honest, path b of the brief): robust per-note pixel geometry is NOT cheaply available, so I did NOT fake it. Why: (1) BOTH engines are black-box CLI subprocesses; the worker reads only the `.musicxml` file (see `run_oemer`/`run_clarity` in worker.py). Neither returns bboxes through that interface. Recovering oemer's internal NoteHead bboxes or Clarity's YOLO staff/system boxes would mean modifying the engines (separate venvs) = the large refactor the brief ruled out. (2) The engine MusicXML carries NO layout coordinates (no `default-x`/`default-y`/`<print>` - confirmed on `public/demo.musicxml` and the engine output shape). (3) The worker has ZERO geometry code (no staff-line/barline/system detection anywhere). Fallback (a) (onset->x + staff->y-band) needs a from-scratch system-detection + logical-measure-to-visual-system assignment + barline pipeline on the stitched multi-page raster; getting the measure assignment wrong (pickup bars, multi-system pages, page breaks inside the stitched PNG) yields a PLAUSIBLE WRONG crop that could clear the 0.10 margin and mis-arbitrate, which violates never-worse-than-Clarity. The Slice-5 decline-on-bad-crop guard protects against DEGENERATE crops, NOT against a clean crop of the WRONG note. So `reconcile._localize_dispute(...)` returns None: the integration is wired + tested end-to-end, the referee is a CORRECT NO-OP (declines on None), and the seam is ready for a real localizer with zero plumbing change.**
  - **What I wired (reconcile.py):** `referee_enabled()` sub-gate (mirrors timing/add helpers: ANDs OMR_ENSEMBLE_REFEREE with parent OMR_ENSEMBLE, truthy `"1"`/`"true"`). `reconcile(primary, secondary, input_pdf=None)` gained an OPTIONAL `input_pdf` (defaulting None keeps every current caller's behavior). In the matched class-B branch: after `_vote_pitch` returns the heuristic winner, if `use_referee` (input_pdf set AND referee_enabled) AND `winner is clarity_ev` (heuristics fell through to the Clarity tiebreak) AND `_pitch_vote_is_residual(...)` AND the slot is isolated, call `_maybe_referee_pitch(...)`. `_pitch_vote_is_residual` is a PURE predicate that mirrors `_vote_pitch`'s exact branch order and returns True ONLY when no heuristic separated the pair (both in range, both diatonic-or-both-not, no octave-jump split, voice-leading tie/absent). `_isolated_slots(events)` = `(measure,staff,onset)` slots holding EXACTLY ONE pitched note (chords/coincident notes excluded; rests are not noteheads). `_maybe_referee_pitch` does the cheap PURE scope gate FIRST (`referee.pitch_interval_semitones` + `is_refereeable_dispute(interval, is_isolated, is_pitch_dispute=True)`) BEFORE any localize/render, lazily `import referee` (so the pure path stays stdlib-only and verovio-less CI is fine), short-circuits on `REFEREE_AVAILABLE False`, then localizes -> renders A=Clarity/B=oemer via `render_candidate` -> `referee_pick`. `'a'`->keep Clarity, `'b'`->oemer wins (adopts ONLY the `<pitch>` via the existing `_apply_pitch`, class B only - never a third pitch, never moves a note), None/anything->decline. Wrapped never-raise (any exception -> decline -> Clarity).**
  - **What I wired (worker.py):** `_select_ensemble` passes the rasterized original (`image_path`, the stitched PNG oemer already consumed) into `_reconcile_paths(clarity_path, oemer_path, workdir, image_path)`. `_reconcile_paths` gained an optional `raster_path` and calls new `_load_referee_raster(raster_path)` which loads a float32 grayscale ndarray ([0,1], 0=ink) via Pillow+numpy ONLY when `reconcile.referee_enabled()` (so NO image decode on every job when the gate is off) and never-raises to None. Then `reconcile.reconcile(primary_bytes, secondary_bytes, input_pdf=input_pdf)`. Gate off -> input_pdf None -> reconcile's referee branch never entered = byte-identical to Slice 4 (verified: with-pdf == without-pdf when off).**
  - **Tests:** `test_reconcile.py` +24 (55 -> ~74 reconcile): referee pick-oemer-wins on a residual in-scope third dispute (E5 vs G5, interval 3); decline keeps Clarity; pick-clarity keeps Clarity; OUT-of-scope step (interval 2) never calls referee_pick; not-residual (diatonicity already decided) never calls referee_pick; chorded/non-isolated slot never calls referee_pick; sub-gate OFF never calls referee_pick; no input_pdf never calls; REFEREE_AVAILABLE False is a no-op; localization None keeps Clarity (the SHIPPED state); referee_pick raising + localization raising both swallowed (never propagate); sub-gate parent-requirement + truthy parsing; PURE unit tests for `_pitch_vote_is_residual` and `_isolated_slots`. Tests stub `referee.render_candidate`+`referee_pick` (+ force REFEREE_AVAILABLE True) and monkeypatch `reconcile._localize_dispute` to a non-None crop, so they need NO verovio and RUN in the base env. `test_worker.py` +4: `_reconcile_paths` passes input_pdf None when referee off (no decode of a bogus raster), loads the array when on (`pytest.importorskip` numpy/PIL), `_load_referee_raster(None)`/decode-failure -> None. `src/omr-worker.test.ts` +1 guard + updated the exact-call guard to `reconcile.reconcile(primary_bytes, secondary_bytes, input_pdf=input_pdf)`; reads reconcile.py as text to assert the sub-gate/helpers exist. RESULTS: base env (no verovio) 143 pytest passed + 16 skipped (15 verovio referee tier from #153 + 1 numpy raster test); `/tmp/verovio-spike` venv 159 passed (nothing skipped, the real scope predicates admit the third dispute). 338 JS + `npm run build` green.**
  - **REMAINING BLOCKER for a non-no-op referee: a reliable `(measure, staff, onset) -> (pdf_crop, staff_geometry)` localizer on the rasterized input. Options when picked up: (a) detect systems + staff lines + barlines on the stitched raster and map logical measures to visual systems (substantial, must handle pickup/multi-system/page-break correctly or it mis-crops); (b) get one engine to emit per-note bboxes (oemer NoteHead bboxes are recoverable internally per the tie-spike, but needs an engine-side change + parsing an extra artifact). Until then the referee is wired, tested, and a guaranteed no-op. The infra side (verovio + libcairo2 + py>=3.11 on the cx33) is DONE per the task note (#153, REFEREE_AVAILABLE=True on the box), so flipping OMR_ENSEMBLE_REFEREE on today is safe but inert.**

- **2026-06-02 - ENSEMBLE OMR SLICE 6 (first sub-slice) BUILT: `omr-worker/referee.py` is the PURE, validated visual-diff referee MATCHING module + `omr-worker/test_referee.py` (branch `feat/omr-referee-module`, NO PR yet). It is NOT wired into worker.py or reconcile.py (mirrors how Slice 2 built reconcile.py pure before Slice 3 wired it). With the code present but uncalled, and verovio not yet on the prod worker, prod is COMPLETELY unaffected. It is a faithful port of the validated throwaway `/tmp/referee_real3.py`.**
  - **Guarded import (the load-bearing safety): the prod worker venv has NO verovio yet.** referee.py wraps `import verovio/cairosvg/numpy/PIL/scipy` in a `try/except Exception` (not just ImportError, so a half-broken native dep like cairocffi failing to dlopen libcairo also degrades) and exposes `REFEREE_AVAILABLE: bool` + `_IMPORT_ERROR`. An ImportError NEVER escapes; every public fn short-circuits to its safe default (None/decline/False) when `REFEREE_AVAILABLE` is False. Verified: with verovio/cairosvg blocked, the module still imports, REFEREE_AVAILABLE=False, referee_pick/render_candidate return None, the pure scope predicates still work.
  - **Public API:** `render_candidate(step, octave, clef="G", alter=0, dpi=350) -> float32 gray ndarray | None` (engrave a minimal one-note/one-measure MusicXML with EMPTY `<part-name>` -> SVG via verovio -> rasterize via cairosvg COMPOSITED ON WHITE first -> grayscale; the dpi scales the cairosvg output_width off the 1600px@350 harness convention). `referee_pick(pdf_crop, staff_geometry, candidate_a, candidate_b) -> 'a'|'b'|None`. `score_candidate(...)`, `is_refereeable_dispute(interval_semitones, is_isolated, is_pitch_dispute) -> bool`, `pitch_interval_semitones(pa, pb)`. `staff_geometry` is `{"lines":[y0..y4], "x_center": notehead_x}` in pdf_crop pixels (caller detects the staff once per system; the referee does NOT re-detect on the original to avoid registration drift).
  - **Method (ported verbatim from the validated harness):** register candidate-to-original by STAFF (align top line + rescale candidate interline to the original's), SUPPRESS the 5 staff-line rows (~0.1 interline band -> white) in BOTH, then NCC over a SMALL HORIZONTAL slide only (+/- ~0.5 interline; NO vertical slide because the pitch dispute IS the vertical position). Candidate notehead localization = rightmost notehead-shaped connected component past a 40%-width clef/meter cutoff, after removing staff-line rows and a vertical binary-close so an open-notehead ring rejoins. Compare INK (1 - gray).
  - **Decline-on-low-margin is the core safety:** `MARGIN_THRESHOLD = 0.10` (Slice 5 real-PDF baseline margins were +0.30..+0.62, so 0.10 leaves wide headroom while declining the noisy/ambiguous cases that erode below it). referee_pick returns the winner ONLY if `abs(score_a - score_b) >= 0.10`, else None. Any None score (render fail, bad crop, registration-height mismatch, degenerate geometry) -> decline. `is_refereeable_dispute` encodes the validated scope as a PURE predicate (no verovio): True only for isolated-notehead PITCH disputes of >= a minor third (`MIN_REFEREEABLE_SEMITONES = 3`); False for steps/2nds (1-2 semitones), duration disputes, and dense/beamed (not isolated). Callers can gate cheaply BEFORE any render.
  - **never-raise contract:** every public fn (and the internal image primitives) wraps work in try/except and returns the safe default; verified with garbage inputs (non-array crop, bad geometry dict, nonsense step/clef).
  - **requirements.txt: added `verovio` + `cairosvg` with comments noting the install constraints (verovio linux-x86_64 manylinux wheel is Python >= 3.11 ONLY; cairosvg needs system libcairo2). Adding them is INERT (module guarded + unwired). The cx33 install + Python >= 3.11 bump is a SEPARATE infra task; do not assume these import on the box yet.** worker.py + reconcile.py BYTE-IDENTICAL to origin/main (confirmed via `git diff --stat`).
  - **Tests (`test_referee.py`, 39 total):** TWO tiers. PURE tier (24 tests: scope predicates, pitch_interval_semitones, the guarded-import degrade path via monkeypatching REFEREE_AVAILABLE False, never-raise on garbage) runs EVERYWHERE incl. a verovio-less CI/prod venv. verovio tier (15 tests, `@pytest.mark.skipif(not REFEREE_AVAILABLE)`) GENERATES the "original" fixture at test time by rendering a known pitch with verovio (stand-in original crop), so the suite is self-contained with NO committed binary fixture: correct beats octave-wrong + third-wrong by >= margin (order-independent), declines on symmetric-wrong (octave-up vs octave-down, third-up vs third-down -> margin < threshold), declines when a candidate fails to render / on degenerate geometry, render compositing is non-blank (not all-black = transparent-bg gotcha handled, not all-white). RESULTS: in the `/tmp/verovio-spike` venv (py3.11, verovio 6.2.1 + cairosvg + scipy; I `pip install`ed pytest into it) all 39 PASSED (the verovio tests RAN, not skipped). With verovio import blocked: 24 passed, 15 SKIPPED cleanly (no failures), confirming CI/prod safety. Same-font self-generated original gives correct-score 1.000 and wrong ~0 (margin ~+1.0), even cleaner separation than the cross-font real PDFs. `npm test` 337 pass + `npm run build` green (untouched by python). reconcile suite still 55 pass. NEXT (Slice 6 cont.): wire referee_pick into reconcile.py as the residual-conflict tiebreaker behind its own sub-gate under OMR_ENSEMBLE (heuristics first, referee only on low-confidence isolated octave/third pitch disputes), AND the infra task to put verovio + libcairo2 + py>=3.11 on the cx33 worker.

- **2026-06-02 - ENSEMBLE OMR SLICE 5 REAL-PDF REFEREE VALIDATION DONE (supersedes/upgrades the synthetic spike's CONDITIONAL GO below). Verdict: GO for the referee (Slice 6), scoped to OCTAVE and THIRD isolated-notehead PITCH disputes on clean PDF input; DECLINE step/2nd disputes and dense/beamed regions. The visual signal on REAL MuseScore-exported PDFs is LARGE and ROBUST, and the synthetic cross-font collapse was a METHOD artifact (tight glyph-crop matching keys on font shape), NOT a real limit: registering by staff + suppressing staff lines + comparing the staff BAND keys on notehead POSITION (= the pitch), which is font- and scan-robust. Throwaway: `/tmp/referee_real3.py` is the final harness, reuses the `/tmp/verovio-spike` venv (py3.11, verovio 6.2.1 + cairosvg + scipy). NOTHING landed in the repo, no PR, worker.py/reconcile.py untouched. This entry is the durable record.**
  - **Test material = the product owner's 4 real MuseScore4 PDFs (icarus, Liminality, the cut that always bleeds, Reverie), all A4, all CLEAN digital engravings in MuseScore's LELAND font (NOT scans). Verovio renders LEIPZIG, so this is a real cross-font test (Leland original vs Leipzig candidate). Copied to /tmp, rasterized page 1 at 350 DPI with pdftoppm (matching the worker). Reverie/Liminality are dense beamed 16th-runs (few isolated heads); Icarus is the cleanest (whole/half notes). 5 ISOLATED noteheads chosen across icarus + liminality + reverie (`the cut` had no clean isolated head on p1).**
  - **GROUND-TRUTH GOTCHA worth keeping: reading pitch by eye off a zoom is error-prone (I miscounted icarus m1 as E5 and m7 as D5; both are actually C5).** The reliable method: detect the 5 staff-line y-centers (rows that are near-full-width ink), interline ~24.1px at 350 DPI for MuseScore default staff size, then OVERLAY a labelled red/blue pitch grid (one diatonic step per half-interline, top treble line = F5) onto the actual PNG and read the notehead center against it (`/tmp/grid_*.png`). Final grid-verified test notes: icarus m7 whole=C5, m17 whole=C5, m18 whole=B4; liminality m4 half=G5; reverie m17 half=A4.
  - **THE METHOD THAT WORKS (and the two that FAILED first, both instructive):** (1) FAIL - full staff-band NCC: the 5 identical horizontal staff lines dominate the correlation and drown the ~few-hundred-pixel notehead, so every candidate scores ~equal (margins all 0.000). (2) FAIL - tight glyph-crop NCC (what the synthetic spike's cross-font control did): keys on Leland-vs-Leipzig SHAPE difference, collapses margins to ~0.08. (3) WORKS - REGISTER candidate-to-original by STAFF (align top line + scale by interline; a pitch dispute IS the vertical position, so do NOT vertical-slide the template), SUPPRESS the 5 staff-line rows in BOTH (set a ~0.1-interline band per line to white), then NCC over a small HORIZONTAL slide only (+/- ~0.5 interline to absorb x error). This makes the score driven by notehead POSITION, which is font- and scan-robust. Candidate notehead localization gotcha: in a one-note measure the meter "4/4" digits are notehead-sized blobs, so "widest blob" picks a digit; take the RIGHTMOST qualifying blob past a ~40%-width clef/meter cutoff, and binary-close vertically first so an OPEN notehead ring split by a removed staff line rejoins. Candidate XML must use an EMPTY `<part-name></part-name>` or the "P" part label contaminates the crop.
  - **NUMBERS (NCC margin = correct minus the candidate; positive = correct wins). Baseline, no perturbation:** all 5/5 CORRECT. Octave margin min +0.384, mean +0.524, max +0.617. Third margin min +0.304, mean +0.489, max +0.600. Per note (m_oct / m_3rd): icarus m7 C5 +0.617/+0.600; icarus m17 C5 +0.607/+0.591; icarus m18 B4 +0.611/+0.576; liminality m4 G5 +0.403/+0.373; reverie m17 A4 +0.384/+0.304. (Whole notes on icarus score highest absolute ~0.55; half notes ~0.36-0.41 because their up-stem adds non-position ink. All clear of any sane threshold.)
  - **ROBUSTNESS (the honest stress tests, the make-or-break):** (a) X-JITTER +/-8px (a third of an interline): 25/25 CORRECT, octave margin stays >=+0.303, third >=+0.303 - the horizontal slide absorbs x-registration error fully. (b) Y-REGISTRATION JITTER +/-6px (a quarter interline; the dangerous axis since pitch IS vertical): 23/25 CORRECT. OCTAVE survives everywhere (margin stays >=+0.170 even at the worst dy). THIRD survives almost everywhere (2 WRONG only at dy=+6 on m18/liminality, where the third got confused; octave stayed right). STEP/2nd disputes go NEGATIVE at dy>=+6 (e.g. -0.070, -0.041) - confirming the design's prediction that 1-interline disputes are too tight; DECLINE them. (c) SCAN DEGRADATION (gaussian blur up to 2.5 + noise up to 0.12 on the original crop): 20/20 CORRECT; blur slightly HELPS (smooths the cross-font shape mismatch so position dominates). At heaviest degradation octave stays >=+0.44, third >=+0.39. So the clean-PDF result is NOT fragile to scan-like noise on this method.
  - **GO/NO-GO: GO for Slice 6**, scoped to: OCTAVE pitch disputes (rock-solid: huge margin, survives all perturbations) and THIRD/larger pitch disputes (strong: degrades only under combined large vertical-misregistration, so pair it with a conservative margin threshold and decline-on-low-margin). NO-GO / explicitly DECLINE: STEP (2nd) pitch disputes (margin erodes to negative under a quarter-interline vertical error), all DURATION disputes (out of scope, weak pixel signal), and dense/beamed/overlapping regions (the synthetic spike already showed a third inside a beamed run fails when the wrong head slides onto a neighbor; not re-tested here since all 4 real PDFs' isolated heads were chosen to AVOID dense runs - so Slice 6 must keep the "isolated notehead only" gate the design specifies). The earlier spike's worry that cross-font would collapse real margins is REFUTED for THIS method (position-based, not shape-based); margins on real Leland-vs-Leipzig are +0.3 to +0.6, not +0.08. Slice 6 build per the design entry: pure `omr-worker/referee.py` behind its own sub-gate under `OMR_ENSEMBLE`, default OFF, never-raise, residual-conflict tiebreaker only (heuristics first), decline-on-low-margin (suggested threshold: require correct to beat best wrong by a clear margin, e.g. >=0.10, and only fire on isolated octave/third pitch disputes). Slice 6's first task should still confirm the verovio manylinux wheel + libcairo2 IMPORT on the actual cx33 box (per the spike entry's wheel facts: worker python must be >=3.11), but the SIGNAL question is now answered YES.

- **2026-06-02 - ENSEMBLE OMR SLICE 5 (THROWAWAY FEASIBILITY SPIKE for the free visual-diff PDF referee) DONE. Verdict: CONDITIONAL GO, leaning cautious. The tooling is free + headless + tiny, and the visual-match signal IS real and separable on isolated noteheads when candidate and scan glyphs are similar; BUT a cross-font control (original engraved in a DIFFERENT music font than the candidate, simulating a real scan) collapses the margins to near-noise, so the referee must be tightly scoped + high-threshold + re-validated on a REAL scanned PDF on cx33 in Slice 6 before it is trusted. Scratch code lived in `/tmp/referee_spike.py` + a `/tmp/verovio-spike` venv; NOTHING landed in the repo, no PR, worker.py/reconcile.py untouched. This entry is the durable record.**
  - **GOAL A (tooling) = PASS, free + headless + offline.** `verovio==6.2.1` (LGPLv3, compatible with our GPL-3.0 Clarity dep) engraves MusicXML -> SVG with DISPLAY unset, no Qt/X, no network, no API key, no cap. Footprint 25 MB (negligible vs the ~1.5 GB torch/onnxruntime engine venvs; lives in its own env). Engrave is sub-second. WHEEL FACTS (verified from PyPI JSON): wheels start at **cp310, NOT cp39** (the PyPI summary text falsely claims cp39 - the actual `urls` list does not). The cx33 (x86-64) wheel `manylinux2014_x86_64.manylinux_2_17_x86_64` exists for **cp311-cp314 only** (cp310 has macOS+aarch64 but NOT linux-x86_64), so the worker MUST run Python >= 3.11 for verovio on cx33. macOS arm64 wheels exist cp310-cp314. GOTCHA that cost time: system python on this mac is 3.9.6 -> pip silently fell back to the sdist and tried to build from source (failed: needs swig). Fix = use python3.11. Slice 6 must pin/confirm the worker venv python >= 3.11 and that the manylinux wheel imports on the actual cx33 box.
  - **SVG -> PNG: the design's "reuse pdftoppm/Pillow" path does NOT work; CairoSVG is REQUIRED.** Verovio has no PNG output (only `renderToSVG`), Pillow cannot read SVG, and there is no system SVG rasterizer (no rsvg-convert/inkscape). So SVG->PNG needs `cairosvg` (the design's stated fallback). It installed cleanly and rasterizes fine. cairosvg pulls `cairocffi` (PURE-PYTHON, dlopens system libcairo at runtime) + `cffi` (has linux wheels). So Slice 6 requirements.txt needs `cairosvg`, and the cx33 cloud-init needs `apt-get install libcairo2` (small, free system lib) since cairocffi has no bundled cairo. RASTERIZE GOTCHA: cairosvg renders a TRANSPARENT background and Verovio's SVG has no white bg rect, so a naive `.convert("L")` turns the whole page BLACK (everything reads as ink). Must composite onto white first (`background_color="white"` + paste-on-white-via-alpha). This zeroed every score until fixed; any real referee must do the same.
  - **GOAL B (is the visual signal real?) = REAL but FRAGILE. Metric = normalized cross-correlation (NCC) via slide-to-best template match of the candidate glyph crop into the original onset-slot crop; SSIM as a much-weaker fallback.** HONESTY CAVEAT baked into the spike: we have NO real scanned icarus PDF locally (the repo has only `public/demo.musicxml`; `~/Downloads/icarus*` are unrelated audio stems), so the "original page" was a Verovio render DEGRADED to imitate a scan (downscale->upscale resolution loss, gaussian blur, additive gaussian noise, sub-pixel affine shift, contrast push). A real scanned PDF on cx33 is the missing validation Slice 6 must add.
  - **Numbers, isolated noteheads (original = degraded SAME-font Verovio), NCC correct vs wrong:** octave G4-vs-G5 +0.338, G4-vs-G3 +0.746, C5-vs-C6 +0.758; third E5-vs-G5 +0.292, A4-vs-F4 +0.285; step E5-vs-F5 +0.161, B4-vs-A4 +0.194. 8/9 pitch cases separate by >0.05 (min +0.161 once the dense case is excluded). Octave separation SURVIVES 8 varied scan degradations (margin min +0.333, mean +0.339, all >0.05) - robust to registration/scan noise in the same-font regime. SSIM on the SAME third-error case was only +0.058 vs NCC's +0.292, confirming the design's "NCC primary, SSIM fallback" call: SSIM alone is borderline.
  - **WHERE IT IS NOISY (matches the design's predictions):** (1) DENSE/ADJACENT material: a third error (E5 vs G5) inside a BEAMED stepwise eighth-note run FAILED (margin +0.000) even with a tightened central-slot crop, because the wrong notehead slides onto a NEIGHBOR notehead at nearly the same y and matches equally well. The octave error in the SAME busy run still separated (+0.214 wide crop, +0.107 tight) because an octave is far enough not to coincide with a neighbor. So: confident on isolated noteheads and on LARGE intervals (octaves); unreliable on small intervals in dense/beamed runs. (2) DURATION: half-vs-whole (+0.831), quarter-vs-eighth (+0.559), dotted-quarter-vs-quarter (+0.508) all separated here, but that is because the rest-fill of the remaining bar + flag/notehead-fill change many pixels; a duration difference that does NOT change the glyph or surrounding fill stays the design's predicted weak case and was not cleanly isolated. Regardless, scope the referee to PITCH only.
  - **THE LOAD-BEARING CAVEAT (cross-font control):** when the ORIGINAL is engraved in a DIFFERENT Verovio music font (Petaluma) than the candidate (Leipzig) - a partial stand-in for a real scan using a non-Verovio engraver - the absolute NCC drops from ~0.97 to ~0.26 AND the margins COLLAPSE: third +0.068, octave +0.083, step +0.008. The step-error margin (+0.008) would NOT survive noise. This means the strong same-font margins are partly an artifact of Verovio-vs-Verovio glyph identity; on a real scan the separation will be MUCH tighter and the referee needs (a) a high confidence/margin threshold tuned on REAL scans, (b) strict scoping to octave / large-interval pitch disputes (drop step-level disputes - too small a margin), (c) decline-on-low-margin as the default. SSIM is not strong enough to be primary.
  - **GO/NO-GO: CONDITIONAL GO.** Build Slice 6 (the referee module behind its own sub-gate, default OFF, never-raise, decline-on-low-margin) because the signal is genuinely separable on the dispute type the design already scoped it to (isolated/large-interval pitch). BUT the very first task in Slice 6 is to RE-RUN this experiment against a REAL scanned PDF on cx33 (verovio manylinux wheel import + a true scan crop), because the cross-font control shows real-scan margins are far tighter than the same-font spike suggests. If the real-scan octave/large-interval margin does not clear a conservative threshold with room to spare, STOP and ship the heuristic ensemble as the product. Keep the referee a pure tiebreaker on residual low-confidence conflicts only, never the first arbiter, with Clarity as the fallback. Suggested initial scope: octave + >=third isolated-notehead pitch disputes; explicitly DECLINE on dense/beamed regions and all duration disputes.

- **2026-06-02 - ENSEMBLE OMR SLICE 4 IMPLEMENTED (branch `feat/omr-reconcile-risky`, NOT merged, NO PR yet): the two RISKIEST conflict classes (D timing + C oemer-only ADD) that Slice 3 left as `TODO(slice4)` no-ops are now implemented in `omr-worker/reconcile.py`, each behind its OWN env sub-gate so QA can disable either independently. Both default OFF and both ALSO require `OMR_ENSEMBLE`; with just `OMR_ENSEMBLE=1` (post-Slice-3 behavior) C/D stay no-ops. The never-worse-than-Clarity invariant is preserved: every correction tiebreaks to Clarity and any failure degrades to the Slice-3 behavior (keep Clarity), never throws. Worker flow UNCHANGED (reconcile SELF-gates the sub-classes via env), so `worker.py`, `test_worker.py` flow guards, and `src/omr-worker.test.ts` structural guards needed no flow edits.**
  - **Two new sub-gates (in reconcile.py, NOT worker.py): `OMR_ENSEMBLE_TIMING` gates class D; `OMR_ENSEMBLE_ADD` gates the class-C oemer-only ADD. Both default OFF.** New helpers `timing_enabled()` / `add_enabled()` mirror `worker.ensemble_enabled` truthy parsing (`"1"`/`"true"`, case-insensitive) and AND it with a local `ensemble_enabled()` (reconcile re-reads `OMR_ENSEMBLE` itself so a stray `OMR_ENSEMBLE_TIMING=1` with `OMR_ENSEMBLE` unset is a no-op; the helpers are honest standalone). They live in reconcile.py (not worker) so reconcile self-gates and stays stdlib-only/boto3-free; the worker reconcile call site is untouched.
  - **Class D (timing mismatch), `_resolve_timing` + `_apply_timing`:** a D pair is a SAME-pitch, SAME-(measure,staff) note the engines placed at onsets differing beyond eps, so `align()` bucketed Clarity's copy into only_a and oemer's into only_b (they never matched). We pick the onset that makes the bar metrically complete vs `<time>`, tiebreak Clarity, and ONLY apply in ONE provably-surgical shape: the Clarity note is the LAST note in its cell AND immediately preceded by a `<rest>` (cell is `[rest, note]`). Moving the note = resizing just that leading rest, which shifts NOTHING after it (nothing follows). Apply only when oemer's onset makes the note end EXACTLY at capacity AND Clarity's current onset does NOT (else ambiguous -> keep Clarity), and the resized rest stays positive. ANY other shape (note not last, no leading rest, fractional native ticks, complete-already) -> DECLINE. Declining is always acceptable; corrupting a measure is not. D pairs are CONSUMED (whether applied or declined) so the class-C ADD never re-adds a D-paired oemer note as a fabrication. GOTCHA: NoteEvent has no parent ref and ElementTree has no getparent(), so `_resolve_timing` builds a one-shot `id(note)->measure` map from the primary root for `_apply_timing` to resize the right sibling rest.
  - **Class C oemer-only ADD, `_resolve_oemer_only_adds` + `_maybe_add_oemer_note` + `_insert_into_silence`:** biased HARD toward NOT adding. Add an oemer note ONLY if ALL of: diatonic vs `<fifths>`, in MIDI 21..108, AND it fills a GENUINE empty slot without overflow (the onset holds no PITCHED Clarity note - a Clarity `<rest>` counts as fillable silence, not occupancy - and pitched_fill + dur <= capacity). When adding, the note CONSUMES silence so following onsets never shift: it replaces a `<rest>` at the target onset (shrink the rest by the note's dur, or remove it if it becomes 0), or appends into trailing slack. Onset-on-a-pitched-note or a too-short rest -> DROP. The inserted element is SYNTHESIZED minimal (deep-copy oemer's `<pitch>` only + duration scaled into the CLARITY document's native base), NEVER oemer's whole `<note>` (same Slice-3 fidelity rule: oemer's native duration base / `<staff>` / shape markup must not leak in). GOTCHA: `align()` MATCHES a Clarity rest to a coincident oemer pitched note (rest-vs-note lands in `matched`, pitch None vs pitch differ), so those never reach only_b; reconcile's matched loop now COLLECTS those oemer notes into `rest_slot_adds` and feeds `only_b + rest_slot_adds` to the gated ADD resolver. Clarity-only notes (only_a) are ALWAYS kept (better recall), even when non-diatonic; we never drop a Clarity note.
  - **Tests:** `test_reconcile.py` +15 (40 -> 55): sub-gate no-ops with only `OMR_ENSEMBLE` on, sub-gate-requires-parent, truthy parsing; class D metric-completeness shifts the note / ambiguous keeps Clarity / unsafe shape (note not last) declined / later notes not shifted; class C add when diatonic+fills-gap+in-range (lands at the right slot, Clarity-base duration), dropped when non-diatonic / out-of-range / would-overflow, Clarity-only kept by default + kept-when-suspicious, robust on malformed secondary. `test_worker.py` +2 (95 -> 97 pytest total): drive the REAL reconcile through `worker._reconcile_paths` to confirm ADD is a no-op with only `OMR_ENSEMBLE` and activates with `OMR_ENSEMBLE_ADD`. 97 pytest + 337 JS + build green. Slice-3's 40 reconcile tests + all worker flow/JS guards pass unchanged (default-off = byte-identical to Slice 3). NEXT: Slice 5 (Verovio referee feasibility spike) per the design entry below, OR QA validation of Slices 3-4 on real scores before flipping any gate on by default.

- **2026-06-02 - SLICE 3 CODE REVIEW: two BLOCKING swap-fidelity bugs found + fixed on `feat/omr-reconcile-wire` before merge (PR #151). Both came from the original `_replace_element` emitting oemer's WHOLE `<note>` element (deepcopy + swap) into the Clarity skeleton. That dragged in oemer-native, base-relative markup and could make the output WORSE than Clarity-alone, violating THE critical invariant. Do NOT reintroduce whole-element swapping.**
  - **Bug 1 (chord membership): a class-B pitch swap dropped/flipped `<chord/>`.** Both engines can read the same chord but list its members in a different order, so a matched disagreeing pair can be Clarity's `<chord/>` MEMBER vs oemer's chord ROOT (no `<chord/>`). Swapping the whole oemer element removed the `<chord/>` marker, turning a chord into two sequential notes and OVERFLOWING the bar (every later onset shifts). Repro confirmed: Clarity C5+F#5(chord member), oemer E5(root)+C5(member) -> old code emitted C5,E5 both non-chord sequential.
  - **Bug 2 (duration base): a class-B OR class-E swap wrote oemer's NATIVE `<duration>` (in oemer's `<divisions>`) into the Clarity document (different base).** oemer almost always uses a different divisions than Clarity (oemer div=16 on icarus; Clarity/music21 differs), so EVERY cross-divisions swap multiplied the note length (e.g. a quarter became a 16-quarter note) and corrupted timing.
  - **Fix (`reconcile.py`):** replaced `_replace_element`/`_build_parent_map` with two SURGICAL in-place edits on the Clarity element. `_apply_pitch(clarity_elem, oemer_elem)`: swaps ONLY the `<pitch>` child (deepcopy), keeps Clarity's duration/`<chord/>`/`<type>`/ties/staff, and drops any stale `<accidental>` display hint so the renderer derives it from the new pitch. `_apply_duration(clarity_ev, oemer_ev)`: writes oemer's winning duration scaled into the CLARITY document's native base (`oemer_common * native_clarity / common_clarity`), requires an EXACT integer (no-op/keep-Clarity otherwise so we never desync), and drops the now-stale `<type>`. A pitch vote changes pitch only; a duration vote writes ticks in the skeleton's own base. The voice-leading anchor now re-reads `target_elem`'s pitch after a possible swap (was approximated as Clarity's pitch; now exact since the swap mutates in place). No more `parent_map` (in-place edits don't need a child->parent map; ElementTree-has-no-getparent is moot when you find the child within its known note element).
  - **Regression tests (`test_reconcile.py` +3, now 80 pytest):** `test_class_b_swap_preserves_clarity_chord_membership` (chord member stays a member after a pitch correction), `test_class_b_swap_keeps_clarity_duration_across_divisions` (clarity div=4 vs oemer div=16, pitch vote keeps dur=4 not 16), `test_class_e_swap_writes_duration_in_clarity_base_across_divisions` (whole-note vote writes 16 in div=4, not oemer's raw 64). All 3 FAIL against the pre-fix code and PASS after. The pre-existing class-B/E tests all used SAME-divisions fixtures (div=4 both sides), which is why they masked Bug 2; new tests deliberately mismatch divisions. 80 pytest + 337 JS + build green. SECURITY: no blocking findings - stdlib `ET.fromstring` does not resolve external entities/DTDs by default (XXE-safe), input is locally-generated engine output not raw upload, no subprocess/network/path-traversal in this slice.

- **2026-06-02 - ENSEMBLE OMR SLICE 3 IMPLEMENTED (branch `feat/omr-reconcile-wire`, NOT merged): `reconcile(primary, secondary) -> bytes` wired into `_select_ensemble` BEHIND `OMR_ENSEMBLE` (default OFF), resolving ONLY the safe conflict classes A/B/E with FREE heuristics. Flag OFF = legacy path UNCHANGED (no reconcile call). Flag ON + both engines = reconcile -> merge_to_grand_staff -> normalize_ties -> put_object. Flag ON + one engine = reconcile is a pass-through (no regression vs Slice 1). CRITICAL safety: every heuristic tiebreaks to Clarity; the output can never be worse than Clarity-alone on Clarity-good inputs.**
  - **`reconcile()` in `omr-worker/reconcile.py` (pure stdlib):** parses the PRIMARY (Clarity) into the tree it will serialize (via new `_events_from_root`, a to_events twin that keeps `.elem` refs pointing into THAT root), lowers the secondary via `to_events`, `align()`s them, and for each MATCHED pair swaps in the winner's REAL `<note>` element (a deepcopy, via a child->parent `_build_parent_map` since ElementTree has no getparent()). It emits Clarity's element on a Clarity win so tie/spelling markup is preserved by construction. Robustness: NEVER raises; returns `primary_bytes` unchanged on ANY failure (malformed primary/secondary, no matches, vote error), and on empty/None secondary (single-engine pass-through).
  - **Class A (agree, same onset+pitch):** keep Clarity's element (no-op). **Class B (pitch mismatch):** `_vote_pitch` in strict order: (1) range hard-reject (MIDI 21..108) - an off-piano pitch loses; (2) key diatonicity vs `<fifths>` (a lone non-diatonic candidate loses; `_diatonic_pitch_classes` = major scale from tonic pc `(fifths*7)%12`); (3) octave/range sanity (prefer the candidate within an octave of the staff tessitura, RH=72/LH=48, when the other is an implausible >= octave jump); (4) voice-leading (smaller interval from the previous same-staff note); (5) tie tiebreak -> Clarity; (6) fallback -> Clarity. **Class E (duration mismatch, same onset+pitch):** `_vote_duration` - Clarity tie-chains ALWAYS win first; else prefer the duration that makes the bar EXACTLY metrically complete vs `<time>` (capacity in common-base ticks = `beats*4*base/beat_type`, skipped if non-integer); else the LONGER duration IF it does not overflow the bar; else Clarity. **Class C (one-engine-only) + Class D (timing mismatch beyond eps):** NO-OP this slice (clear `TODO(slice4)` markers in code): Clarity-only notes stay in the skeleton, oemer-only notes (`only_b`) are IGNORED, class-D notes fall into only_a/only_b and are left Clarity-has-it / oemer-ignored.
  - **GOTCHA caught while writing tests:** the voice-leading test first used C5->C6 vs C5->D5, but the OCTAVE-SANITY prior (step 3) fires before voice-leading (C6 is a >=octave jump from the staff center), so that fixture exercised the wrong heuristic. Rewrote it as A4->G5 vs A4->B4 (both within an octave of center, both diatonic, both in range) so ONLY voice-leading separates them. When testing an ordered heuristic chain, make every earlier prior a TIE so the target prior is actually the decider. Also: the voice-leading anchor (`prev_midi_by_cell`) is approximated as Clarity's pitch (primary), not the swapped winner, since re-reading the swapped element would be circular; documented in code as a safe approximation.
  - **DRY (Slice 2 note addressed):** `worker.py` now `import reconcile` + `from reconcile import _clef_sign`, and `worker._clef_sign_of_part` delegates to `reconcile._clef_sign`. Direction is correct: reconcile stays stdlib-only (no boto3), worker imports FROM it. Verified `python3 -c "import reconcile"` works without boto3.
  - **Wiring:** new `worker.run_primary_engines(clarity_fn, oemer_fn, is_pdf)` returns BOTH engine paths (Slice-1 `select_primary_result` only returned the winner; it is RETAINED + still unit-tested). `_select_ensemble` applies the same Clarity>oemer>homr precedence, then when BOTH paths exist calls `_reconcile_paths` (reads both files, calls `reconcile.reconcile`, writes `reconciled.musicxml`, source becomes `"ensemble"`). `_reconcile_paths` returns None only if the primary is unreadable (caller keeps the raw result); a missing/unreadable secondary degrades to a pass-through.
  - **Tests:** `test_reconcile.py` +16: class-A passthrough, class-B per-heuristic (diatonicity, range reject, voice-leading, all-else-equal->Clarity, both-plausible safety), class-E (metric completeness, Clarity tie-chain wins), class-C oemer-only ignored + Clarity-only kept, class-D timing kept-Clarity, tie+spelling markup survives, malformed/empty/None secondary -> primary passthrough, malformed primary -> unchanged, no-matches -> primary. `test_worker.py`: updated `test_ensemble_pdf_runs_both_engines` (source now `"ensemble"` when both succeed) + 3 new (reconcile-before-merge-before-normalize ORDER guard via a full `process_job` drive with a `_FakeClient`; single-engine = reconcile NOT called; flag-OFF = reconcile NEVER called). 77 pytest pass. `src/omr-worker.test.ts` flow guards updated: the ensemble guard now pins `run_primary_engines` + the in-flow Clarity>oemer precedence, plus a NEW guard asserting reconcile fires only when both paths exist and precedes merge->normalize. 337 JS tests + build green. NEXT (Slice 4): class D timing + the hard-gated oemer-only ADD (class C), still under `OMR_ENSEMBLE`.

- **2026-06-02 - ENSEMBLE OMR SLICE 2 IMPLEMENTED (branch `feat/omr-reconcile-model`, NOT wired into worker.py, NOT merged): the pure analyzable core. New stdlib-only module `omr-worker/reconcile.py` lowers each engine's MusicXML into a comparable `NoteEvent` model (`to_events`) and aligns the two streams into matched/only_a/only_b buckets (`align`). ZERO prod risk: nothing in `process_job` calls it yet; this slice is pure code + tests. xml.etree + math + dataclasses only, NO new dependencies.**
  - **`to_events(xml_bytes, src="") -> list[NoteEvent]`:** `NoteEvent` is a `@dataclass` carrying `measure, onset, staff (1=RH/treble,2=LH/bass), pitch=(step,alter,octave)|None, duration, is_chord, tie:set, src, base, elem`. `elem` is the ORIGINAL `<note>` Element (so a later slice emits the WINNER's real element with its tie/spelling markup, never re-synthesizes) and is `compare=False`/`repr=False` so events compare on musical content only. `alter` is an int defaulting to 0, so "C" and explicit `<alter>0</alter>` compare equal. Cursor math generalizes worker `_measure_duration` to track POSITION: a non-chord note advances the cursor by its `<duration>`; a `<chord/>` member shares the PREVIOUS note's onset and does NOT advance; `<backup>`/`<forward>` move the cursor (backup clamps at 0). Robustness contract matches the post-transforms: returns `[]` on ANY parse failure (malformed XML, empty/garbage, structurally surprising doc), NEVER raises.
  - **Time-base normalization (the load-bearing part):** the two engines use different `<divisions>`. `to_events` first scales a document onto its OWN lcm-of-divisions base (handles per-part AND per-measure divisions changes: `_divisions_in` re-reads each measure's `<attributes>/divisions`, which persists until re-declared). The resolved base is RECORDED on `NoteEvent.base`. `align` then rescales BOTH streams onto `lcm(base_a, base_b)` so onsets are directly comparable integers. KEY GOTCHA I hit + fixed: I first recovered the per-stream base via gcd of onsets/durations, but a sub-beat note (a 1-tick jitter/forward in a divisions=8 doc) drives the gcd to 1 and mis-inflates that stream on rescale, breaking the eps match. Carrying the real base explicitly on the event is EXACT; do not go back to gcd recovery.
  - **Staff mapping:** oemer notes carry `<staff>` (read directly, clamped to {1,2}); Clarity's 2 parts have no `<staff>`, so a part's default staff is its FIRST clef sign (G->1, F->2). `_clef_sign` mirrors worker `_clef_sign_of_part`; it is RE-DEFINED in reconcile.py rather than imported because importing worker.py pulls in boto3 (worker imports it at module load), and reconcile must stay importable/testable with stdlib only. Intended DRY direction: worker.py imports `_clef_sign` FROM reconcile in a later slice, not the reverse.
  - **`align(events_a, events_b) -> {matched:[(a,b)], only_a, only_b}`:** group both streams by (measure, staff) cell, then GREEDY nearest-onset match within each cell (tolerance `eps = EPS_BEATS(=1/8 beat) * common_base`, min 1 tick), tie-broken by exact-pitch preference so a coincident same-pitch note beats a same-onset different-pitch note (chord-order independence). A matched pair may DISAGREE on pitch (both engines placed a note in the slot, read it differently): that intentionally lands in `matched` for a LATER voting slice (Slice 3), NOT resolved here. Different staff = different slot = never matches. align copies events before rescaling so it does NOT mutate caller inputs (a test pins this).
  - **Tests:** new `omr-worker/test_reconcile.py` (+21, total pytest now 58 = 37 worker + 21 reconcile). Covers: divisions-mismatch normalization (4 vs 16 still aligns), chord onset sharing + post-chord cursor, backup/forward cursor movement + backup-past-zero clamp, oemer-`<staff>` vs Clarity-clef staff mapping AND cross-shape alignment, alignment buckets (pitch disagreement -> matched, missing -> only_a, extra -> only_b, different-staff -> both unmatched), eps boundary (1-tick jitter matches, half-beat does not), greedy exact-pitch tiebreak, tie/alter parsing, rest -> None pitch, malformed/empty XML -> [] without raising, lcm helpers, equality-ignores-elem, no-mutation. 336 JS tests + build green. `src/omr-worker.test.ts` is UNCHANGED (no worker.py flow change this slice). NEXT (Slice 3): wire `reconcile()` into `process_job` behind `OMR_ENSEMBLE`, default OFF, voting on safe conflict classes A/B/E only.

- **2026-06-02 - ENSEMBLE OMR DESIGN REVISED: pull forward a FREE VISUAL-DIFF PDF REFEREE (no LLM, no paid vision API, still inside the free-tooling rule). The input PDF becomes a first-class TIEBREAKER that arbitrates conflicts the free heuristics cannot confidently resolve, by re-rendering each engine's candidate back to an image and scoring which rendering best matches the original PDF crop. This SUPERSEDES the "PDF-vs-input visual diff is OUT OF SCOPE" line in the 2026-06-02 ensemble DESIGN entry below; everything else in that entry (the reconcile module, NoteEvent model, alignment, conflict taxonomy A-E, heuristic auto-resolution, robustness contract, the post-transform slot) STILL STANDS as prerequisites. Design + revised slice plan recorded here so it is not relitigated. DESIGN ONLY, nothing implemented.**
  - **Renderer choice = VEROVIO (the `verovio` PyPI package), confirmed FREE + headless + no caps.** License LGPL-3.0 / GPL-3.0 (compatible with the GPL-3.0 Clarity-OMR we already ship; no new license risk). It is a self-contained C++ library with prebuilt **manylinux x86-64** wheels (matches the cx33 x86 box) for py3.9-3.13, renders MusicXML -> SVG (and MIDI) entirely OFFLINE/locally, no remote server, no API key, no usage cap. Install footprint is a single small wheel (a few MB) vs the existing ~1.5 GB torch/onnxruntime stack, so it is negligible additive weight and a separate concern from the ML venvs (it can live in the worker's own env; it has no torch/opencv conflict). Speed: Verovio engraves a page in well under a second on CPU, so re-rendering a measure/region is cheap relative to the engines (Clarity ~15s, oemer ~180s). REJECTED alternatives: MuseScore CLI (needs a real Qt/X display or xvfb, heavy GUI bundle, AppImage/Qt deps on a headless server, slow startup) and LilyPond (free + headless but a large TeX-adjacent install, slow per-render, and its input is .ly not MusicXML so it needs a conversion hop). Verovio is the only one that is library-grade headless, MusicXML-native, tiny, and fast.
  - **SVG -> PNG rasterization for the actual pixel compare:** Verovio emits SVG, so the candidate render must be rasterized to a bitmap to diff against the PDF crop. Use **CairoSVG** (pure-Python, free, wraps libcairo which is already a thin system lib) OR route the SVG through the **pdftoppm/Pillow path we ALREADY have installed** (poppler + PIL are on the box, used by `rasterize_if_pdf`/`stitch_pages_vertical`). Prefer reusing pdftoppm+Pillow first (zero new dep) and only add CairoSVG if SVG->PNG fidelity needs it; the spike decides. Either way the comparison happens in numpy/Pillow, no new heavy dep.
  - **Visual-diff method (be honest: this is the noisy part):** the scan and the re-render are NOT pixel-aligned (different DPI, margins, engraving font, spacing, system breaks), so a naive whole-page subtract is meaningless. Approach: (1) REGISTRATION via the structure we already recover, not raw pixels. We already rasterize the PDF at 350 DPI and Clarity/oemer give us per-note bounding-box geometry (the tie-spike proved oemer NoteHead bboxes are recoverable; Clarity carries YOLO system/staff bboxes). Use that geometry to CROP the original PDF raster to the disputed measure or single-note neighborhood, and engrave ONLY that measure/region with Verovio for each candidate, then NORMALIZE both crops to the same height/staff-interline before comparing (scale by detected staff-line spacing so a glyph is the same size in both). (2) SIMILARITY METRIC: for a localized single-glyph dispute, NORMALIZED CROSS-CORRELATION / template matching of the candidate notehead+stem render against the PDF crop at the expected position is the most robust to brightness/threshold differences; SSIM is a reasonable second on a measure-sized crop. Avoid feature-point matching (SIFT/ORB): music glyphs are repetitive and low-texture, feature matching mis-associates identical noteheads. (3) LOCALIZATION: diff the SMALLEST region that isolates the dispute. A pitch dispute = crop a single notehead's vertical neighborhood (the staff position is exactly what differs, so a vertical-band cross-correlation of where the notehead sits vs each candidate's rendered notehead-y is the cleanest signal). A presence dispute (extra/missing note) = crop the onset's horizontal slot in the measure. Whole-measure SSIM is the fallback when single-glyph localization is uncertain. WHERE IT IS NOISY AND CAN MIS-JUDGE: scan skew/warp, beaming and stem-direction differences between Verovio and the original engraver, ledger lines and accidentals shifting glyph extents, dense chords where noteheads overlap, and registration error from imperfect bbox geometry. The referee can confidently pick on a clean isolated notehead pitch dispute; it is unreliable on dense/overlapping material and on rhythm/duration disputes (a duration difference barely changes the pixels at a single onset). So the referee is scoped to the disputes where the visual signal is strong (mainly pitch/octave on isolated noteheads) and explicitly DECLINES (returns "no confident pick", falls back to heuristics) elsewhere.
  - **Integration ordering = HEURISTICS FIRST, referee ONLY on residual conflicts (cheaper + more robust).** The free heuristics from the reconcile design (key-diatonic vote, range/octave sanity, voice-leading, metric completeness, Clarity tiebreak) run FIRST and resolve the large majority of conflicts at ~zero cost. The PDF referee is invoked ONLY for the residual set the heuristics flag as LOW-CONFIDENCE (e.g. a pitch mismatch where both candidates are diatonic and in-range, so the cheap priors do not separate them). This bounds the number of expensive re-render+match operations to a handful per job, not one per disagreement, and means a referee failure can always fall back to the heuristic pick. The referee is a TIEBREAKER, never the first or only arbiter.
  - **Risk + cost + degradation:** (1) LATENCY: each referee call = engrave one region with Verovio (<1s) + rasterize + crop + correlate (tens of ms). With residual-only invocation (a handful of disputes per page) the added wall-clock is a second or two, negligible against oemer's ~180s. The dominant cost stays the engines, not the referee. (2) FALSE ARBITRATION: the referee picking the WRONG candidate because the visual match is noisy is the headline risk (it could swap a correct heuristic/Clarity pick for a worse one). Mitigations: a CONFIDENCE THRESHOLD on the correlation score (the winning candidate must beat the loser by a margin; ties/low-margin = DECLINE and keep the heuristic pick), scope to strong-signal dispute types only, and the whole referee behind its own sub-gate so it can be disabled without touching reconciliation. (3) DEGRADATION STORY (never regress): if Verovio fails to install/import, if engraving raises, if rasterization fails, if the crop/registration is degenerate, or if the match margin is below threshold -> the referee returns "no pick" and the conflict falls back to the FREE HEURISTIC result, which itself falls back to Clarity. Same never-raise-into-process_job contract as reconcile/the post-transforms. So worst case the referee is a no-op and we are exactly at the heuristic-ensemble behavior; it can only ever ADD a confident correction, never subtract reliability.
  - **REVISED SLICE PLAN (re-sliced from here; Slice 1 already shipped in #149; the old reconcile Slices 2-4 are renumbered 2-4 and stand unchanged; the visual referee is added LAST and is spike-gated). Each slice is independently shippable and the risky visual stuff is last + flag-gated:**
    1. **Slice 1 (DONE, #149): run both engines concurrently behind `OMR_ENSEMBLE`, fallback selection unchanged.** Shipped.
    2. **Slice 2 (M, prerequisite, unchanged): `to_events` normalization + comparable NoteEvent model + `align()` buckets in `omr-worker/reconcile.py`, not wired in.** (Old Slice 2.)
    3. **Slice 3 (M, prerequisite, unchanged): reconcile SAFE conflict classes (A AGREE, B PITCH, E DURATION) behind `OMR_ENSEMBLE`, default OFF, heuristics only.** (Old Slice 3.)
    4. **Slice 4 (M, prerequisite, unchanged): timing (class D) + hard-gated oemer-only ADD (class C).** (Old Slice 4.)
    5. **Slice 5 (S, THROWAWAY-ABLE FEASIBILITY SPIKE, do this BEFORE committing to the referee): prove the renderer + the visual match on ONE real disputed example.** Scratch code under `/tmp` (NOT wired into worker.py, NOT shipped). Goals: (a) `pip install verovio` succeeds and `verovio` imports + engraves a MusicXML measure to SVG HEADLESS on the cx33 worker (and SVG->PNG via pdftoppm/Pillow or CairoSVG works there); (b) take ONE real disputed note from a real score (the icarus test PDF, where we KNOW the ground-truth pitch) and show the cross-correlation/template score for the CORRECT candidate render beats the WRONG candidate render against the original PDF crop, by a clear margin. DELIVERABLE = a yes/no on "is the visual signal real and separable on real material." If NO (signal too noisy to separate correct from wrong reliably), STOP: do not build the referee, the heuristic ensemble is the product. Only proceed to Slice 6 if the spike shows clear separation.
    6. **Slice 6 (M, only if Slice 5 passes): the referee module + integration, behind its own sub-gate under `OMR_ENSEMBLE`, default OFF.** New pure module (e.g. `omr-worker/referee.py`): given the original PDF raster, a dispute (measure/staff/onset + the two candidate elements), engrave each candidate region with Verovio, rasterize, register/crop, correlate, return a confident pick or None. Wire it into reconcile as the residual-conflict tiebreaker (heuristics first, referee only on low-confidence). Never-raise contract; below-margin = decline. Test surface: pure scoring fn unit tests, decline-on-failure, decline-on-low-margin, the integration only firing on residual conflicts.
    7. **Slice 7 (S): after QA validates Slices 3-6 on real scores, flip the gates ON by default; kill-switches stay.** Gated on QA, not just CI.
  - **Files this will touch (beyond the reconcile files in the entry below):** new `omr-worker/referee.py` + `omr-worker/test_referee.py`; `omr-worker/worker.py` (Verovio in the worker env, referee call inside the reconcile residual path, the referee sub-gate); `omr-worker/requirements.txt` (add `verovio`, and `cairosvg` only if the spike shows pdftoppm/Pillow SVG handling is insufficient); `omr-worker/hetzner-cloud-init.yaml` (install verovio so a fresh VM has it). The engines, post-transforms, and the browser correction UI are UNCHANGED.

- **2026-06-02 - ENSEMBLE OMR SLICE 1 FLAG-GATED (branch `feat/omr-ensemble-parallel`, NOT yet merged): the concurrent path now ships behind `OMR_ENSEMBLE` (default OFF) so Slice 1 is TRULY zero-risk in prod. FLAG OFF (= prod today) keeps the legacy Clarity-first SHORT-CIRCUIT byte- AND latency-identical to current main; FLAG ON uses the concurrent `select_primary_result` path. This fixes a latency regression the always-concurrent version would have shipped: before the flag, every prod PDF went from ~15s (Clarity short-circuit) to ~max(clarity, oemer) ~180s for ZERO user benefit, because reconciliation is not wired until Slice 3.**
  - **The flag (`omr-worker/worker.py`):** new `OMR_ENSEMBLE_ENV = "OMR_ENSEMBLE"` + pure `ensemble_enabled()` helper (truthy = `"1"`/`"true"`, case-insensitive, whitespace-tolerant; unset / `"0"` / `"false"` / anything else = OFF). Read in exactly one place so every later slice (reconciliation) reuses it. `process_job` now branches: `if ensemble_enabled(): _select_ensemble(...) else: _select_legacy(...)`, both returning `(result_path, source)` before the shared post-transform + put_object block.
  - **`_select_legacy` (flag OFF, prod default):** restores the pre-ensemble flow EXACTLY. Clarity is PRIMARY and SHORT-CIRCUITS for a PDF: if `run_clarity` succeeds, oemer is NOT run and the PDF is NEVER rasterized (so latency stays ~15s). Only on Clarity failure (or for PNG/JPEG where Clarity is skipped) does it rasterize -> oemer -> homr, the original sequential fallback. No upfront rasterization, no concurrency, no per-engine timeout (the legacy runners are called without `timeout=`, matching old main). Verified against `origin/main:omr-worker/worker.py` process_job.
  - **`_select_ensemble` (flag ON):** the concurrent body described directly below (rasterize up front, `select_primary_result` over a ThreadPoolExecutor with per-engine `timeout=engine_timeout_seconds()`, homr last resort, raster-failure-non-fatal-on-PDF). This is the path QA validates with `OMR_ENSEMBLE=1` on the worker BEFORE it ever becomes default, and the slot where reconciliation (Slice 3+) hooks in.
  - **Tests for both modes:** `omr-worker/test_worker.py` +6 (37 pytest total): `ensemble_enabled` truthy/falsy parsing; flag-OFF Clarity-success-does-NOT-run-oemer-or-rasterize (the load-bearing prod guarantee, asserts via runners that raise if called); flag-OFF Clarity-fails -> oemer fallback; flag-OFF PNG skips Clarity; flag-ON both-engines-run (records each call, asserts oemer ran even though Clarity won); flag-ON raster-failure-still-runs-Clarity. The existing `select_primary_result` selector tests (max-not-sum, timeouts, precedence) stand unchanged under the flag-ON path. `src/omr-worker.test.ts` flow guards updated: a flag-gating guard (`OMR_ENSEMBLE_ENV`/`ensemble_enabled`/the `process_job` branch), a legacy-short-circuit guard (rasterize+oemer are INSIDE `if result_path is None:` in `_select_legacy`, so skipped on the Clarity happy path), and the concurrent-precedence guard (now scoped to `_select_ensemble`, since `select_primary_result` + `run_homr` moved out of `process_job`). 336 JS tests + build green.

- **2026-06-02 - ENSEMBLE OMR SLICE 1 IMPLEMENTED (concurrent body, NOW gated by `_select_ensemble` per the flag entry ABOVE): run Clarity + oemer CONCURRENTLY with a per-engine timeout, selection precedence UNCHANGED. ZERO output change for every input; only the SCHEDULING changed (parallel, not Clarity-then-oemer). This is the safe first slice of the ensemble design recorded directly above; reconciliation is still Slice 3+.**
  - **What changed in `omr-worker/worker.py`:** new pure `select_primary_result(run_clarity_fn, run_oemer_fn, is_pdf_input, timeout)` launches the two PRIMARY engines on a `concurrent.futures.ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=2)` and applies the EXACT old precedence: Clarity if it returned a path, else oemer, else None. Threads are correct here because each engine is a `subprocess.run` (GIL released during the OS wait), so wall-clock is ~max(clarity, oemer), not the sum. `process_job` now rasterizes UP FRONT (so oemer's image is ready to run alongside Clarity), then calls the selector, then falls back to `run_homr` only when BOTH primaries failed (homr stays the last-resort engine OUTSIDE the concurrent stage, unchanged). Per-engine timeout: `engine_timeout_seconds()` reads `OMR_ENGINE_TIMEOUT_SECONDS` (default `DEFAULT_ENGINE_TIMEOUT_SECONDS = 1200`, garbage/non-positive -> default); `run_clarity`/`run_oemer`/`run_homr` now take `timeout=` and pass it to `subprocess.run`, converting `subprocess.TimeoutExpired` into None (engine "failed", degrade to survivor) exactly like the existing CalledProcessError path.
  - **Behavior-preservation subtlety (do not regress):** the OLD PDF flow short-circuited at Clarity and NEVER rasterized when Clarity succeeded; the NEW flow always rasterizes so oemer can run concurrently.
